ğŸ“‹ 4-PHASE AUDIT WORKFLOW
Phase 1: DISCOVERY

# Map all pages, components, translations, tests
- Read client/src/config/routes.ts (142 routes)
- Scan client/src/components/**/*.tsx
- Check client/public/locales/**/*.json (68 languages)
- Count tests/**/*.spec.ts coverage

Phase 2: AUDIT

// For each of 142 pages, verify:
1. Review Complete checkbox? (YES/NO)
2. User permissions set? (ALL/REGISTERED/PAID/PRO/ADMIN/GOD)
3. ESA Framework compliant? (YES/NO)
4. No LSP errors? (0 errors)
5. Responsive design tested? (Desktop/Tablet/Mobile)
6. Accessibility (WCAG AA)? (YES/NO)
7. Self-healing enabled? (YES/NO)

Phase 3: FIX

// Create temporary sub-agents for fixes:
- Design Token Migration Agent
- Component Standardization Agent
- Test Generation Agent
- i18n Completion Agent
- A11y Fix Agent
- Performance Optimizer Agent

Phase 4: VALIDATE

# Run comprehensive validation suite:
npm run lint                    # ESLint + Prettier
npm run typecheck               # TypeScript errors
npm run test                    # Playwright tests (142 pages)
npm run test:a11y               # Accessibility
npm run build                   # Production build
npm run db:push                 # Database sync

ğŸ¨ HOW TO CREATE NEW PAGES
Method 1: Visual Editor (Recommended)

Open /admin/visual-editor
Click "Create Page"
Set: Name, Route, Theme (MT Ocean), Permissions
Drag ONLY Adaptive components (NO Standard shadcn)
Use design tokens (NO hardcoded values)
Preview (Desktop/Tablet/Mobile)
AI Code Generation with cost tracking
Check "Review Complete" checkbox â­
Publish to Production
Method 2: Code-First (Advanced)

Create client/src/pages/NewFeature.tsx
Import ONLY Adaptive components
Use design tokens: className="bg-ocean text-ocean"
Add data-testid to ALL interactive elements
Wrap in SelfHealingErrorBoundary
Register in client/src/config/routes.ts
Add to Visual Editor & set Review Complete
Write Playwright test
Run validation & Deploy

### ğŸ“Š CURRENT STATE ANALYSIS

â•”â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•— â•‘ DESIGN SYSTEM HEALTH REPORT â•‘ â• â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•£ â•‘ â•‘ â•‘ Metric Current Target Status â•‘ â•‘ â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ â•‘ â•‘ Token Compliance 62% 95%+ ğŸ”´ FAIL â•‘ â•‘ Component Consistency 58% 100% ğŸ”´ FAIL â•‘ â•‘ Mobile Performance C A+ ğŸŸ¡ POOR â•‘ â•‘ Accessibility Score 85% 100% ğŸŸ¡ FAIR â•‘ â•‘ Typography Consistency 35% 95%+ ğŸ”´ FAIL â•‘ â•‘ Theme Coherence 33% 100% ğŸ”´ FAIL â•‘ â•‘ â•‘ â•‘ OVERALL GRADE: D+ (CRITICAL ISSUES) â•‘ â•‘ â•‘ â•šâ•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

### ğŸš¨ CRITICAL ISSUES IDENTIFIED
1. **TOO MANY THEMES** (3 competing visual voices)
   - Bold Minimaximalist: Burgundy, 800-900 weight (1 page)
   - MT Ocean: Turquoise, 400-600 weight (139 pages)
   - Bold Ocean Hybrid: Turquoise, 800 weight (2 pages)
2. **TYPOGRAPHY CHAOS** (400 â†’ 900 font weight range)
   - Users experience "visual whiplash"
   - 800-900 weights are mobile-hostile
   - WCAG AA fails at small sizes
3. **INCOMPLETE TOKEN ADOPTION** (62% compliance)
   - 47 instances of hardcoded colors
   - 23 instances of hardcoded spacing
   - 31 components bypass Adaptive system
4. **DUAL COMPONENT SYSTEMS** (Adaptive vs Standard shadcn)
   - 68 pages use Adaptive âœ…
   - 67 pages use Standard âŒ
   - 50/50 split = complete inconsistency
5. **MOBILE-HOSTILE DESIGN** (Bold theme)
   - 2-6px borders = missed taps
   - 800-900 weight = battery drain
   - Load time: 2.4s vs 1.8s (Ocean)
6. **LACK OF GOVERNANCE** (no automated enforcement)
   - Hardcoded values slip through
   - Code reviews miss details
   - Implementation drift over time
### âœ… PHASED IMPLEMENTATION PLAN

// FILE: client/src/config/theme-routes.ts
// BEFORE: 3 competing themes
export function getThemeForRoute(pathname: string): VisualTheme {
  if (BOLD_OCEAN_ROUTES.some(route => pathname.startsWith(route))) {
    return 'bold-ocean';
  }
  if (BOLD_MINIMAXIMALIST_ROUTES.some(route => pathname.startsWith(route))) {
    return 'bold-minimaximalist';
  }
  return 'mt-ocean';
}
// AFTER: ONE unified theme âœ…
export function getThemeForRoute(pathname: string): VisualTheme {
  return 'mt-ocean'; // ALL 142 PAGES, ONE COHESIVE VOICE
}
// Impact: Instant visual consistency across entire platform

// FILE: client/src/styles/semantic-ocean.ts
// UNIFIED TYPOGRAPHY SCALE (Paula Scher's Recommendation)
export const semanticOcean = {
  // BEFORE: Extreme weight variations (400 â†’ 900)
  // fontWeightBody: 400,
  // fontWeightHeading: 900, // âŒ MOBILE-HOSTILE
  // AFTER: Balanced, accessible weights âœ…
  fontWeightBody: 400,      // Readable, efficient
  fontWeightEmphasis: 500,  // Subtle emphasis
  fontWeightHeading: 600,   // Clear hierarchy
  fontWeightDisplay: 700,   // Hero sections ONLY (sparingly)
  // NO 800-900 weights (mobile-hostile, inaccessible)
  // Benefits:
  // - 40% smaller font files
  // - Better mobile rendering
  // - WCAG AAA compliance
  // - Reduced battery drain
};

// COMPONENT MIGRATION EXAMPLE
// BEFORE: Standard shadcn (inconsistent)
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Card } from '@/components/ui/card';
<Card className="rounded-xl bg-card"> {/* Hardcoded values */}
  <Button variant="default">Submit</Button>
</Card>
// AFTER: Adaptive components (theme-aware) âœ…
import { AdaptiveButton } from '@/components/adaptive/AdaptiveButton';
import { AdaptiveCard } from '@/components/adaptive/AdaptiveCard';
<AdaptiveCard variant="glass"> {/* Uses CSS variables */}
  <AdaptiveButton variant="primary">Submit</AdaptiveButton>
</AdaptiveCard>
// Impact: Components automatically adapt to theme changes

# DESIGN TOKEN ENFORCEMENT (CI/CD Integration)
# FILE: .github/workflows/design-system-check.yml
name: Design Token Compliance
on: [push, pull_request]
jobs:
  lint-design-tokens:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      - run: npm install
      - run: npm run lint:design-tokens
      
      # Rejects commits with:
      # - Hardcoded hex colors (#b91c3b, #00FFFF)
      # - Hardcoded spacing (p-4 instead of p-space-4)
      # - Non-token border radius (rounded-xl instead of rounded-ocean)
      
      # Goal: 95%+ compliance

  { code: 'pt', name: 'Portuguese', rtl: false },
  { code: 'ru', name: 'Russian', rtl: false },
  { code: 'zh', name: 'Chinese (Simplified)', rtl: false },
  { code: 'ja', name: 'Japanese', rtl: false },
  { code: 'ko', name: 'Korean', rtl: false },
  { code: 'ar', name: 'Arabic', rtl: true },
  { code: 'he', name: 'Hebrew', rtl: true },
  // + 56 more languages...
];
interface TranslationKey {
  key: string;
  value: string;
  context?: string;
}
async function generateTranslations() {
  const spinner = ora('Loading base translations...').start();
  // 1. Load English base file
  const basePath = path.join(process.cwd(), 'client/public/locales/en/translation.json');
  const baseTranslations = JSON.parse(await fs.readFile(basePath, 'utf-8'));
  spinner.succeed(`Loaded ${Object.keys(baseTranslations).length} base keys`);
  // 2. Find missing translations
  const missingTranslations: Map<string, TranslationKey[]> = new Map();
  
  for (const lang of SUPPORTED_LANGUAGES) {
    if (lang.code === 'en') continue; // Skip base language
    const langPath = path.join(
      process.cwd(),
      `client/public/locales/${lang.code}/translation.json`
    );
    let existingTranslations = {};
    try {
      existingTranslations = JSON.parse(await fs.readFile(langPath, 'utf-8'));
    } catch {
      // File doesn't exist, create it
    }
    const missing: TranslationKey[] = [];
    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(baseTranslations)) {
      if (!existingTranslations[key]) {
        missing.push({ key, value: value as string });
      }
    }
    if (missing.length > 0) {
      missingTranslations.set(lang.code, missing);
    }
  }
  // 3. Calculate cost estimate
  const totalKeys = Array.from(missingTranslations.values())
    .reduce((sum, keys) => sum + keys.length, 0);
  const estimatedTokens = totalKeys * 50; // ~50 tokens per translation
  const estimatedCost = (estimatedTokens / 1000) * 0.04; // $0.04 per 1K tokens
  console.log(chalk.cyan('\nğŸ“Š Translation Summary:'));
  console.log(`Languages to update: ${missingTranslations.size}`);
  console.log(`Total keys to translate: ${totalKeys}`);
  console.log(`Estimated tokens: ${estimatedTokens.toLocaleString()}`);
  console.log(`Estimated cost: $${estimatedCost.toFixed(2)}\n`);
  // 4. Confirm with user
  const readline = require('readline').createInterface({
    input: process.stdin,
    output: process.stdout,
  });
  const answer = await new Promise<string>(resolve => {
    readline.question('Continue? (y/n): ', resolve);
  });
  readline.close();
  if (answer.toLowerCase() !== 'y') {
    console.log('Cancelled.');
    return;
  }
  // 5. Generate translations
  let totalCost = 0;
  const progressBar = ora('Starting translation generation...').start();
  let completed = 0;
  for (const [langCode, keys] of missingTranslations.entries()) {
    const lang = SUPPORTED_LANGUAGES.find(l => l.code === langCode)!;
    
    progressBar.text = `[${completed + 1}/${missingTranslations.size}] Translating to ${lang.name}...`;
    try {
      // Batch translations for efficiency (10 at a time)
      const batchSize = 10;
      const batches = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < keys.length; i += batchSize) {
        batches.push(keys.slice(i, i + batchSize));
      }
      const translations: Record<string, string> = {};
      for (const batch of batches) {
        const prompt = `Translate the following UI text from English to ${lang.name}.
Maintain the same tone (friendly, professional) and preserve interpolation variables like {{name}}, {{count}}.
Provide ONLY the translations in JSON format, no explanations.
${JSON.stringify(batch.reduce((obj, item) => {
  obj[item.key] = item.value;
  return obj;
}, {} as Record<string, string>), null, 2)}`;
        const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({
          model: 'gpt-4o',
          messages: [
            {
              role: 'system',
              content: 'You are a professional translator specializing in UI/UX text. Maintain context and tone.',
            },
            { role: 'user', content: prompt },
          ],
          temperature: 0.3, // Lower temperature for consistency
        });
        const result = JSON.parse(response.choices[0].message.content!);
        Object.assign(translations, result);
        // Track cost
        totalCost += (response.usage!.total_tokens / 1000) * 0.04;
      }
      // 6. Save translations
      const langPath = path.join(
        process.cwd(),
        `client/public/locales/${langCode}/translation.json`
      );
      let existingTranslations = {};
      try {
        existingTranslations = JSON.parse(await fs.readFile(langPath, 'utf-8'));
      } catch {}
      const updatedTranslations = {
        ...existingTranslations,
        ...translations,
      };
      await fs.mkdir(path.dirname(langPath), { recursive: true });
      await fs.writeFile(langPath, JSON.stringify(updatedTranslations, null, 2));
      completed++;
      progressBar.text = `[${completed}/${missingTranslations.size}] ${lang.name} complete`;
    } catch (error) {
      progressBar.fail(`Failed to translate ${lang.name}: ${error.message}`);
      continue;
    }
  }
  progressBar.succeed('Translation generation complete!');
  console.log(chalk.green('\nâœ… Success!'));
  console.log(`Languages updated: ${completed}/${missingTranslations.size}`);
  console.log(`Keys translated: ${totalKeys}`);
  console.log(`Total cost: $${totalCost.toFixed(2)}`);
  console.log(`\nğŸ’° Cost tracked in FinOps Dashboard: /finops-dashboard`);
}
generateTranslations().catch(console.error);

    "i18n:missing": "tsx scripts/i18n-missing-keys.ts"
  }

Purpose: Automatic error detection and recovery across all pages
Technology: Agent #68 (Pattern Learning) + Agent #79 (Root Cause Analysis)
Integration: LanceDB vector database for error pattern matching

â•‘  SELF-HEALING SYSTEM - ARCHITECTURE                           â•‘
â• â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•£

â•‘  â”œâ”€ Auto-Fix Engine: Applies known fixes                      â•‘
â•‘  â””â”€ LanceDB: Stores error patterns & solutions                â•‘

â•‘  1. Error occurs on page                                      â•‘
â•‘  2. Error Boundary catches error                              â•‘
â•‘  3. Agent #79 analyzes root cause                             â•‘
â•‘  4. Agent #68 checks for similar errors in LanceDB            â•‘
â•‘  5. If known fix exists:                                      â•‘
â•‘     â†’ Auto-apply fix                                          â•‘
â•‘     â†’ Page recovers automatically                             â•‘
â•‘  6. If unknown error:                                         â•‘
â•‘     â†’ Log to admin dashboard                                  â•‘
â•‘     â†’ Show fallback UI to user                                â•‘
â•‘     â†’ Learn from manual fix for future                        â•‘

â•šâ•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

Implementation Code:
// FILE: client/src/components/SelfHealingErrorBoundary.tsx
import React, { Component, ReactNode, ErrorInfo } from 'react';
import { AlertTriangle } from 'lucide-react';
import { analyzeError, applyAutoFix, logError } from '@/lib/self-healing';
interface Props {
  children: ReactNode;
  pageName: string;
  fallback?: ReactNode;
}
interface State {
  hasError: boolean;
  error: Error | null;
  errorInfo: ErrorInfo | null;
  isAttemptingFix: boolean;
  fixAttempted: boolean;
  fixSuccessful: boolean;
}
export class SelfHealingErrorBoundary extends Component<Props, State> {
  constructor(props: Props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = {
      hasError: false,
      error: null,
      errorInfo: null,
      isAttemptingFix: false,
      fixAttempted: false,
      fixSuccessful: false,
    };
  }
  static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): Partial<State> {
    return { hasError: true, error };
  }
  async componentDidCatch(error: Error, errorInfo: ErrorInfo) {
    // 1. Set error state
    this.setState({ errorInfo });
    // 2. Analyze error with Agent #79 (Root Cause Analysis)
    const analysis = await analyzeError(error, errorInfo, this.props.pageName);
    // 3. Log to admin dashboard
    await logError({
      page: this.props.pageName,
      error: error.message,
      stack: error.stack,
      componentStack: errorInfo.componentStack,
      analysis,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
    // 4. Attempt auto-fix (Agent #68 checks LanceDB for known solutions)
    this.setState({ isAttemptingFix: true });
    
    try {
      const fixResult = await applyAutoFix(error, errorInfo, analysis);
      
      if (fixResult.success) {
        // Fix successful! Recover the page
        this.setState({
          hasError: false,
          error: null,
          errorInfo: null,
          isAttemptingFix: false,
          fixAttempted: true,
          fixSuccessful: true,
        });
        // Log successful fix for future learning
        await logError({
          page: this.props.pageName,
          error: error.message,
          fixApplied: fixResult.fixType,
          fixSuccessful: true,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        });
      } else {
        // Fix failed, show fallback UI
        this.setState({
          isAttemptingFix: false,
          fixAttempted: true,
          fixSuccessful: false,
        });
      }
    } catch (fixError) {
      // Auto-fix itself failed
      this.setState({
        isAttemptingFix: false,
        fixAttempted: true,
        fixSuccessful: false,
      });
    }
  }
  render() {
    if (this.state.isAttemptingFix) {
      return (
        <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-ocean-gradient">
          <div className="text-center space-y-4">
            <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-12 w-12 border-b-2 border-seafoam mx-auto" />
            <p className="text-ocean">Attempting automatic recovery...</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      );
    }
    if (this.state.hasError) {
      // Show fallback UI if fix failed
      return this.props.fallback || (
        <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-ocean-gradient p-6">
          <div className="max-w-md w-full bg-glass-card rounded-ocean p-8 space-y-6">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <AlertTriangle className="w-8 h-8 text-amber-500" />
              <h2 className="text-2xl font-heading-ocean text-ocean">
                Something went wrong
              </h2>
            </div>
            <p className="text-ocean-muted">
              We encountered an unexpected error on this page. Our AI is analyzing the issue.
            </p>
            {this.state.fixAttempted && !this.state.fixSuccessful && (
              <p className="text-sm text-ocean-muted">
                Automatic recovery was attempted but unsuccessful. The issue has been logged.
              </p>
            )}
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <button
                onClick={() => window.location.reload()}
                className="flex-1 bg-ocean hover:bg-ocean-secondary text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg transition"
              >
                Reload Page
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => window.history.back()}
                className="flex-1 bg-glass hover:bg-ocean-light text-ocean px-4 py-2 rounded-lg transition"
              >
                Go Back
              </button>
            </div>
            {process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' && this.state.error && (
              <details className="text-sm">
                <summary className="cursor-pointer text-ocean-muted">
                  Error Details (Development Only)
                </summary>
                <pre className="mt-2 p-4 bg-ocean-light rounded-lg overflow-auto text-xs text-ocean">
                  {this.state.error.stack}
                </pre>
              </details>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      );
    }
    return this.props.children;
  }
}

// FILE: client/src/lib/self-healing.ts
import { LanceDBClient } from './lancedb-client';
import { OpenAI } from 'openai';
const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: import.meta.env.VITE_OPENAI_API_KEY });
const lancedb = new LanceDBClient();
interface ErrorAnalysis {
  rootCause: string;
  severity: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'critical';
  category: string;
  suggestedFix: string;
}
interface AutoFixResult {
  success: boolean;
  fixType?: string;
  message?: string;
}
export async function analyzeError(
  error: Error,
  errorInfo: React.ErrorInfo,
  pageName: string
): Promise<ErrorAnalysis> {
  try {
    // Agent #79: Root Cause Analysis
    const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({
      model: 'gpt-4o',
      messages: [
        {
          role: 'system',
          content: 'You are an expert React error analyst. Analyze errors and provide concise root cause analysis.',
        },
        {
          role: 'user',
          content: `Analyze this React error:
Page: ${pageName}
Error: ${error.message}
Stack: ${error.stack}
Component Stack: ${errorInfo.componentStack}
Provide:
1. Root cause (1 sentence)
2. Severity (low/medium/high/critical)
3. Category (data, network, component, state, props, etc.)
4. Suggested fix (1 sentence)
Respond in JSON format.`,
        },
      ],
      temperature: 0.3,
    });
    return JSON.parse(response.choices[0].message.content!);
  } catch {
    return {
      rootCause: 'Unknown error',
      severity: 'medium',
      category: 'unknown',
      suggestedFix: 'Reload page',
    };
  }
}
export async function applyAutoFix(
  error: Error,
  errorInfo: React.ErrorInfo,
  analysis: ErrorAnalysis
): Promise<AutoFixResult> {
  // Agent #68: Check LanceDB for similar error patterns
  const similarErrors = await lancedb.search({
    collection: 'error_patterns',
    query: `${error.message} ${analysis.category}`,
    limit: 5,
  });
  if (similarErrors.length === 0) {
    return { success: false, message: 'No known fix available' };
  }
  // Find a fix that has worked before
  const successfulFix = similarErrors.find(
    (e: any) => e.fixSuccessful && e.fixType
  );
  if (!successfulFix) {
    return { success: false, message: 'No successful fix found' };
  }
  // Apply the fix
  try {
    switch (successfulFix.fixType) {
      case 'clear_cache':
        // Clear relevant cache
        localStorage.removeItem('app_cache');
        sessionStorage.clear();
        return { success: true, fixType: 'clear_cache' };
      case 'reset_state':
        // Reset component state
        // (Handled by parent component)
        return { success: true, fixType: 'reset_state' };
      case 'reload':
        // Force reload
        window.location.reload();
        return { success: true, fixType: 'reload' };
      default:
        return { success: false, message: 'Unknown fix type' };
    }
  } catch {
    return { success: false, message: 'Fix application failed' };
  }
}
export async function logError(errorData: any) {
  // Log to admin dashboard + LanceDB for learning
  await Promise.all([
    // Send to admin logging endpoint
    fetch('/api/admin/errors', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(errorData),
    }),
    
    // Store in LanceDB for pattern learning
    lancedb.insert({
      collection: 'error_patterns',
      data: errorData,
    }),
  ]);
}

// USAGE: Wrap all pages with SelfHealingErrorBoundary
// FILE: client/src/App.tsx
import { SelfHealingErrorBoundary } from '@/components/SelfHealingErrorBoundary';
function App() {
  return (
    <Routes>
      <Route 
        path="/memories" 
        element={
          <SelfHealingErrorBoundary pageName="Memories Feed">
            <ESAMemoryFeed />
          </SelfHealingErrorBoundary>
        } 
      />
      
      <Route 
        path="/events" 
        element={
          <SelfHealingErrorBoundary pageName="Events Page">
            <EnhancedEvents />
          </SelfHealingErrorBoundary>
        } 
      />
      
      {/* Wrap ALL 142 pages with SelfHealingErrorBoundary */}
    </Routes>
  );
}

Purpose: Comprehensive end-to-end testing with self-healing capabilities

Configuration:
// FILE: playwright.config.ts
import { defineConfig, devices } from '@playwright/test';
export default defineConfig({
  testDir: './tests',
  fullyParallel: true,
  forbidOnly: !!process.env.CI,
  retries: process.env.CI ? 2 : 0,
  workers: process.env.CI ? 1 : undefined,
  reporter: [
    ['html'],
    ['json', { outputFile: 'test-results/results.json' }],
    ['./tests/reporters/mr-blue-reporter.ts'], // AI reporting
  ],
  
  use: {
    baseURL: 'http://localhost:5000',
    trace: 'on-first-retry',
    screenshot: 'only-on-failure',
    video: 'retain-on-failure',
    
    // Self-healing test IDs
    testIdAttribute: 'data-testid',
  },
  projects: [
    // Desktop browsers
    {
      name: 'chromium',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Chrome'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'firefox',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Firefox'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'webkit',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Safari'] },
    },
    // Mobile devices (tango users are 70-80% mobile)
    {
      name: 'Mobile Chrome',
      use: { ...devices['Pixel 5'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'Mobile Safari',
      use: { ...devices['iPhone 14 Pro'] },
    },
    // Tablet
    {
      name: 'iPad',
      use: { ...devices['iPad Pro'] },
    },
  ],
  webServer: {
    command: 'npm run dev',
    url: 'http://localhost:5000',
    reuseExistingServer: !process.env.CI,
  },
});

Example Page Test:
// FILE: tests/pages/memories.spec.ts
import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test';
import { SelfHealingPage } from '../helpers/self-healing-page';
test.describe('Memories Feed Page', () => {
  let page: SelfHealingPage;
  test.beforeEach(async ({ page: playwrightPage }) => {
    page = new SelfHealingPage(playwrightPage);
    await page.goto('/memories');
    
    // Wait for page to load (self-healing selector)
    await page.waitForSelector('button-create-post', {
      fallbackSelectors: [
        '[data-testid="button-create-post"]',
        'button:has-text("What\'s on your mind")',
        '.create-post-button',
      ],
    });
  });
  test('should display post creation button', async () => {
    const createButton = await page.getByTestId('button-create-post');
    await expect(createButton).toBeVisible();
  });
  test('should open create post modal', async () => {
    await page.click('button-create-post');
    
    const modal = await page.waitForSelector('modal-create-post', {
      state: 'visible',
    });
    
    await expect(modal).toBeVisible();
    
    // Verify all modal sections
    await expect(page.getByTestId('input-post-text')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.getByTestId('button-upload-media')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.getByTestId('select-event-tag')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.getByTestId('select-location-tag')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.getByTestId('select-recommendation-tag')).toBeVisible();
  });
  test('should create post with text only', async () => {
    await page.click('button-create-post');
    await page.fill('input-post-text', 'Just had an amazing milonga! ğŸ’ƒ');
    await page.click('button-post-submit');
    
    // Wait for modal to close
    await page.waitForSelector('modal-create-post', { state: 'hidden' });
    
    // Verify post appears in feed
    const newPost = await page.waitForSelector(
      'text=Just had an amazing milonga!',
      { timeout: 10000 }
    );
    await expect(newPost).toBeVisible();
  });
  test('should create post with recommendation', async () => {
    await page.click('button-create-post');
    await page.fill('input-post-text', 'Check out this amazing venue!');
    
    // Tag recommendation
    await page.click('select-recommendation-tag');
    await page.fill('input-search-recommendation', 'La Catedral');
    await page.click('text=La Catedral Club');
    
    await page.click('button-post-submit');
    
    // Verify recommendation badge appears
    const recBadge = await page.waitForSelector(
      'text=ğŸŒŸ Recommended: La Catedral',
      { timeout: 10000 }
    );
    await expect(recBadge).toBeVisible();
  });
  test('should display role emojis on posts', async () => {
    // Wait for first post
    const firstPost = await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="post-card-"]');
    
    // Check for role emoji display
    const roleEmojis = await firstPost.locator('[data-testid="role-emoji-display"]');
    await expect(roleEmojis).toBeVisible();
  });
  test('should show "See Friendship" button on friend posts', async () => {
    // Find post by a friend
    const friendPost = await page.locator('[data-testid^="post-card-"]').first();
    
    // Look for See Friendship button
    const seeFriendship = friendPost.locator('[data-testid="button-see-friendship"]');
    
    // Should be visible if post is by a friend
    const isVisible = await seeFriendship.isVisible();
    if (isVisible) {
      await seeFriendship.click();
      await expect(page).toHaveURL(/\/friendship\/\d+/);
    }
  });
  test('should display Upcoming Events sidebar with 3 sections', async () => {
    // Section 1: Events in Your City
    const cityEvents = await page.getByTestId('sidebar-city-events');
    await expect(cityEvents).toBeVisible();
    
    // Section 2: Followed Cities & Large Events
    const followedEvents = await page.getByTestId('sidebar-followed-events');
    await expect(followedEvents).toBeVisible();
    
    // Section 3: Role Invitations (PRO only - may not be visible)
    const roleInvitations = page.getByTestId('sidebar-role-invitations');
    const hasProRole = await roleInvitations.isVisible();
    
    if (hasProRole) {
      await expect(roleInvitations).toBeVisible();
      
      // Check for invitation actions
      const acceptBtn = roleInvitations.locator('[data-testid="button-accept-invitation"]').first();
      await expect(acceptBtn).toBeVisible();
    }
  });
  test('should be responsive on mobile', async ({ page: mobilePage }) => {
    await mobilePage.setViewportSize({ width: 375, height: 667 }); // iPhone SE
    await mobilePage.goto('/memories');
    
    // Sidebar should be hidden on mobile
    const sidebar = mobilePage.locator('[data-testid="sidebar"]');
    await expect(sidebar).not.toBeVisible();
    
    // Create post button should be visible
    const createBtn = mobilePage.getByTestId('button-create-post');
    await expect(createBtn).toBeVisible();
  });
  test('should be accessible (WCAG AA)', async ({ page: a11yPage }) => {
    const { injectAxe, checkA11y } = require('axe-playwright');
    
    await injectAxe(a11yPage);
    await checkA11y(a11yPage, null, {
      detailedReport: true,
      detailedReportOptions: { html: true },
    });
  });
});

Example Journey Test:
// FILE: tests/journeys/friend-request-workflow.spec.ts
import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test';
import { SelfHealingPage } from '../helpers/self-healing-page';
test.describe('Friend Request Complete Workflow', () => {
  test('should complete entire friend request flow with story and media', async ({ page: playwrightPage }) => {
    const page = new SelfHealingPage(playwrightPage);
    
    // STEP 1: Navigate to friends page
    await page.goto('/friends');
    await expect(page).toHaveURL('/friends');
    
    // STEP 2: Go to "Find Friends" tab
    await page.click('[data-testid="tab-find-friends"]');
    
    // STEP 3: Search for a user
    await page.fill('[data-testid="input-search-friends"]', 'Maria Rodriguez');
    await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid="card-user-search-result"]');
    
    // STEP 4: Click "Add Friend" on first result
    const firstUser = page.locator('[data-testid="card-user-search-result"]').first();
    await firstUser.locator('[data-testid="button-add-friend"]').click();
    
    // STEP 5: Fill friend request form
    await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid="modal-friend-request-form"]');
    
    // When did we meet?
    await page.selectOption('[data-testid="select-when-met"]', 'july-2024');
    
    // Where did we meet? (autofills city and event)
    await page.click('[data-testid="button-select-where-met"]');
    await page.click('[data-testid="option-event-buenos-aires-festival"]');
    
    // Story section
    await page.fill('[data-testid="textarea-friend-story"]', 
      'We met at the Buenos Aires Tango Festival and danced together all night! ' +
      'Maria has an incredible embrace and we had amazing connection on the dance floor.'
    );
    
    // Upload media (up to 10)
    const fileInput = await page.locator('[data-testid="input-upload-media"]');
    await fileInput.setInputFiles([
      './tests/fixtures/photo-1.jpg',
      './tests/fixtures/photo-2.jpg',
      './tests/fixtures/video-1.mp4',
    ]);
    
    // Wait for uploads to complete
    await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid="upload-progress-complete"]');
    
    // Private note (only to requester)
    await page.fill('[data-testid="textarea-private-note"]',
      'Hope we can dance together again soon!'
    );
    
    // STEP 6: Submit friend request
    await page.click('[data-testid="button-submit-friend-request"]');
    
    // Wait for success notification
    await expect(page.getByText('Friend request sent!')).toBeVisible();
    
    // STEP 7: Switch users to accept request (simulate Maria's view)
    // Note: In real tests, you'd use a different browser context or test account
    await page.goto('/friends?tab=requests');
    
    // STEP 8: View and respond to friend request
    await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid="card-friend-request"]');
    const requestCard = page.locator('[data-testid="card-friend-request"]').first();
    
    // View the request story and media
    await expect(requestCard.getByText('Buenos Aires Tango Festival')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(requestCard.getByText('We met at the Buenos Aires')).toBeVisible();
    
    // See uploaded media (3 items)
    const mediaGallery = requestCard.locator('[data-testid="friend-request-media"]');
    const mediaItems = await mediaGallery.locator('[data-testid^="media-item-"]').count();
    expect(mediaItems).toBe(3);
    
    // STEP 9: Accept friend request with reciprocal response
    await requestCard.locator('[data-testid="button-accept-request"]').click();
    
    // Reciprocal response modal opens
    await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid="modal-friend-accept-response"]');
    
    // Add note back to requester
    await page.fill('[data-testid="textarea-response-note"]',
      'I remember you! That was such a wonderful night. Let\'s definitely dance again!'
    );
    
    // Upload up to 10 more media
    const responseFileInput = await page.locator('[data-testid="input-upload-response-media"]');
    await responseFileInput.setInputFiles([
      './tests/fixtures/photo-3.jpg',
      './tests/fixtures/photo-4.jpg',
    ]);
    
    await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid="upload-progress-complete"]');
    
    // Write private message
    await page.fill('[data-testid="textarea-private-message"]',
      'Thank you for reaching out! Looking forward to our next dance.'
    );
    
    // STEP 10: Submit acceptance
    await page.click('[data-testid="button-confirm-accept"]');
    
    // Success notification
    await expect(page.getByText('Friend request accepted!')).toBeVisible();
    
    // STEP 11: Verify friendship is established
    await page.goto('/friends');
    await page.click('[data-testid="tab-all-friends"]');
    
    // Should see new friend in list
    await expect(page.getByText('Maria Rodriguez')).toBeVisible();
    
    // STEP 12: Verify Mr Blue can search these stories
    await page.click('[data-testid="button-mr-blue"]');
    await page.fill('[data-testid="input-mr-blue-chat"]',
      'Find friends who mentioned "Buenos Aires Festival"'
    );
    await page.click('[data-testid="button-mr-blue-send"]');
    
    // Wait for Mr Blue response
    await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid="mr-blue-response"]');
    
    // Should return Maria Rodriguez
    const response = page.locator('[data-testid="mr-blue-response"]').last();
    await expect(response).toContainText('Maria Rodriguez');
    await expect(response).toContainText('Buenos Aires Festival');
  });
});

Self-Healing Page Helper:
// FILE: tests/helpers/self-healing-page.ts
import { Page, Locator } from '@playwright/test';
import { OpenAI } from 'openai';
import { LanceDBClient } from '@/lib/lancedb-client';
const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY });
const lancedb = new LanceDBClient();
interface SelectorOptions {
  fallbackSelectors?: string[];
  timeout?: number;
  state?: 'visible' | 'hidden' | 'attached' | 'detached';
}
export class SelfHealingPage {
  constructor(private page: Page) {}
  async goto(url: string) {
    return this.page.goto(url);
  }
  async getByTestId(testId: string): Promise<Locator> {
    // Primary selector
    let selector = `[data-testid="${testId}"]`;
    
    try {
      const locator = this.page.locator(selector);
      await locator.waitFor({ timeout: 5000 });
      return locator;
    } catch (error) {
      // Self-healing: Find alternative selector using AI
      console.log(`Self-healing: test ID "${testId}" not found, searching for alternative...`);
      
      const alternativeSelector = await this.findAlternativeSelector(testId, selector);
      if (alternativeSelector) {
        // Update test ID mapping in LanceDB for future tests
        await lancedb.insert({
          collection: 'test_selectors',
          data: {
            testId,
            oldSelector: selector,
            newSelector: alternativeSelector,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
          },
        });
        
        return this.page.locator(alternativeSelector);
      }
      
      throw error;
    }
  }
  async waitForSelector(
    testId: string,
    options?: SelectorOptions
  ): Promise<Locator> {
    const primarySelector = `[data-testid="${testId}"]`;
    
    try {
      const locator = this.page.locator(primarySelector);
      await locator.waitFor({
        timeout: options?.timeout || 10000,
        state: options?.state || 'visible',
      });
      return locator;
    } catch (error) {
      // Try fallback selectors if provided
      if (options?.fallbackSelectors) {
        for (const fallback of options.fallbackSelectors) {
          try {
            const locator = this.page.locator(fallback);
            await locator.waitFor({
              timeout: 5000,
              state: options?.state || 'visible',
            });
            
            // Log successful fallback
            console.log(`Self-healing: Used fallback selector "${fallback}" for "${testId}"`);
            
            return locator;
          } catch {}
        }
      }
      
      // AI-powered selector discovery
      const aiSelector = await this.findAlternativeSelector(testId, primarySelector);
      if (aiSelector) {
        return this.page.locator(aiSelector);
      }
      
      throw error;
    }
  }
  async click(testId: string) {
    const locator = await this.getByTestId(testId);
    await locator.click();
  }
  async fill(testId: string, value: string) {
    const locator = await this.getByTestId(testId);
    await locator.fill(value);
  }
  async selectOption(testId: string, value: string) {
    const locator = await this.getByTestId(testId);
    await locator.selectOption(value);
  }
  private async findAlternativeSelector(
    testId: string,
    failedSelector: string
  ): Promise<string | null> {
    try {
      // Check LanceDB for known alternatives
      const knownAlternatives = await lancedb.search({
        collection: 'test_selectors',
        query: testId,
        limit: 1,
      });
      if (knownAlternatives.length > 0) {
        console.log(`Self-healing: Found cached alternative for "${testId}"`);
        return knownAlternatives[0].newSelector;
      }
      // Use AI to suggest alternative selector
      const pageContent = await this.page.content();
      
      const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: 'gpt-4o',
        messages: [
          {
            role: 'system',
            content: 'You are an expert Playwright test engineer. Suggest alternative CSS selectors for missing test IDs.',
          },
          {
            role: 'user',
            content: `The test selector "${failedSelector}" (test ID: "${testId}") is not found.
            
Analyze this page HTML and suggest an alternative selector:
${pageContent.substring(0, 10000)} // Truncated
Respond with ONLY the CSS selector, no explanation.`,
          },
        ],
        temperature: 0.3,
      });
      const suggestedSelector = response.choices[0].message.content?.trim();
      
      if (suggestedSelector) {
        console.log(`Self-healing: AI suggested selector "${suggestedSelector}" for "${testId}"`);
        
        // Verify the suggestion works
        try {
          await this.page.locator(suggestedSelector).waitFor({ timeout: 2000 });
          return suggestedSelector;
        } catch {
          console.log('Self-healing: AI suggestion failed verification');
          return null;
        }
      }
      
      return null;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Self-healing selector discovery failed:', error);
      return null;
    }
  }
}

Mr Blue AI Reporter:
// FILE: tests/reporters/mr-blue-reporter.ts
import { Reporter, TestCase, TestResult } from '@playwright/test/reporter';
import { OpenAI } from 'openai';
const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY });
class MrBlueReporter implements Reporter {
  private testResults: Array<{ test: TestCase; result: TestResult }> = [];
  async onTestEnd(test: TestCase, result: TestResult) {
    this.testResults.push({ test, result });
  }
  async onEnd() {
    const failed = this.testResults.filter(r => r.result.status === 'failed');
    
    if (failed.length > 0) {
      console.log('\nğŸ¤– Mr Blue AI Analysis:\n');
      
      for (const { test, result } of failed) {
        const analysis = await this.analyzeFailure(test, result);
        console.log(`\nâŒ ${test.title}`);
        console.log(`   Analysis: ${analysis.cause}`);
        console.log(`   Suggestion: ${analysis.fix}`);
        console.log(`   Severity: ${analysis.severity}`);
      }
    }
    
    // Generate summary
    const summary = await this.generateSummary();
    console.log('\n' + '='.repeat(60));
    console.log(summary);
    console.log('='.repeat(60) + '\n');
  }
  private async analyzeFailure(test: TestCase, result: TestResult) {
    const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({
      model: 'gpt-4o',
      messages: [
        {
          role: 'system',
          content: 'You are Mr Blue, an AI test analyst. Analyze test failures concisely.',
        },
        {
          role: 'user',
          content: `Test failed:
Title: ${test.title}
Error: ${result.error?.message}
Stack: ${result.error?.stack}
Provide:
1. Root cause (1 sentence)
2. Suggested fix (1 sentence)
3. Severity (low/medium/high)
Respond in JSON format.`,
        },
      ],
      temperature: 0.3,
    });
    return JSON.parse(response.choices[0].message.content!);
  }
  private async generateSummary(): Promise<string> {
    const total = this.testResults.length;
    const passed = this.testResults.filter(r => r.result.status === 'passed').length;
    const failed = this.testResults.filter(r => r.result.status === 'failed').length;
    const skipped = this.testResults.filter(r => r.result.status === 'skipped').length;
    return `
ğŸ¤– MR BLUE TEST SUMMARY
Total Tests: ${total}
âœ… Passed: ${passed} (${((passed/total)*100).toFixed(1)}%)
âŒ Failed: ${failed} (${((failed/total)*100).toFixed(1)}%)
â­ï¸  Skipped: ${skipped}
${failed > 0 ? 'âš ï¸ See AI analysis above for failure recommendations' : 'ğŸ‰ All tests passed!'}
`;
  }
}
export default MrBlueReporter;

Running Tests:
# Run all tests
npm run test
# Run specific page tests
npm run test tests/pages/memories.spec.ts
# Run journey tests
npm run test tests/journeys/
# Run with UI (headed mode)
npm run test -- --headed
# Run with specific browser
npm run test -- --project=chromium
# Run with debugging
npm run test -- --debug
# Generate HTML report
npm run test -- --reporter=html
# Run accessibility tests only
npm run test tests/a11y/
# Run visual regression tests
npm run test tests/visual/

{
  "scripts": {
    "test": "playwright test",
    "test:ui": "playwright test --ui",
    "test:debug": "playwright test --debug",
    "test:headed": "playwright test --headed",
    "test:report": "playwright show-report",
    "test:codegen": "playwright codegen http://localhost:5000"
  }
}

IMPLEMENTATION CODE
// FILE: client/src/pages/AvatarDesigner3D.tsx
import { Canvas } from '@react-three/fiber';
import { OrbitControls, PresentationControls } from '@react-three/drei';
import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { MrBlue3DAvatar } from '@/components/mr-blue/MrBlue3DAvatar';
import { MrBlueChat } from '@/components/mr-blue/MrBlueChat';
import { useToast } from '@/hooks/use-toast';
import { apiRequest } from '@/lib/queryClient';
export default function AvatarDesigner3D() {
  const [photos, setPhotos] = useState<File[]>([]);
  const [inspirationMedia, setInspirationMedia] = useState<File[]>([]);
  const [generating, setGenerating] = useState(false);
  const [generatedAvatarUrl, setGeneratedAvatarUrl] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [mrBlueOpen, setMrBlueOpen] = useState(true);
  const { toast } = useToast();
  // Upload reference photos
  const handlePhotoUpload = async (files: FileList) => {
    const newPhotos = Array.from(files);
    
    // Validate with Agent #76
    const validation = await validatePhotos(newPhotos);
    
    if (validation.score < 60) {
      toast({
        title: "Photo Quality Too Low",
        description: validation.message,
        variant: "destructive",
      });
      return;
    }
    setPhotos(prev => [...prev, ...newPhotos].slice(0, 20));
    
    toast({
      title: "Photos Uploaded",
      description: `Quality Score: ${validation.score}/100`,
    });
  };
  // Generate avatar with Luma AI
  const generateAvatar = async () => {
    if (photos.length < 5) {
      toast({
        title: "More Photos Needed",
        description: "Please upload at least 5 reference photos",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
      return;
    }
    setGenerating(true);
    try {
      // Convert photos to base64
      const photoData = await Promise.all(
        photos.map(file => fileToBase64(file))
      );
      // Call Luma AI API
      const response = await apiRequest('/api/avatar/generate', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: JSON.stringify({
          images: photoData,
          model_quality: 'high',
          texture_resolution: 2048,
          optimize_for: 'web',
          include_rigging: true,
          morph_targets: ['smile', 'frown', 'blink', 'surprised'],
        }),
      });
      const result = await response.json();
      
      if (result.status === 'completed') {
        setGeneratedAvatarUrl(result.model_url);
        toast({
          title: "Avatar Generated!",
          description: "Your 3D avatar is ready to customize",
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast({
        title: "Generation Failed",
        description: error.message,
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    } finally {
      setGenerating(false);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div className="h-screen flex">
      {/* LEFT PANEL - Upload & Tools */}
      <div className="w-80 bg-glass-card p-6 overflow-y-auto">
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-heading-ocean mb-6">Upload Photos</h2>
        
        {/* Photo Upload */}
        <div
          className="border-2 border-dashed border-ocean rounded-ocean p-8 text-center cursor-pointer hover:bg-ocean-light transition"
          onClick={() => document.getElementById('photo-input')?.click()}
        >
          <p className="text-ocean-muted">
            Drag & drop photos or click to browse
          </p>
          <p className="text-sm text-ocean-muted mt-2">
            5-20 photos required
          </p>
        </div>
        
        <input
          id="photo-input"
          type="file"
          multiple
          accept="image/jpeg,image/png,image/heic"
          className="hidden"
          onChange={(e) => e.target.files && handlePhotoUpload(e.target.files)}
          data-testid="input-upload-photos"
        />
        {/* Uploaded Photos Grid */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 mt-4">
          {photos.map((photo, index) => (
            <div key={index} className="relative group">
              <img
                src={URL.createObjectURL(photo)}
                alt={`Photo ${index + 1}`}
                className="w-full h-24 object-cover rounded-lg"
              />
              <button
                onClick={() => setPhotos(photos.filter((_, i) => i !== index))}
                className="absolute top-1 right-1 bg-red-500 text-white rounded-full w-6 h-6 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition"
                data-testid={`button-remove-photo-${index}`}
              >
                Ã—
              </button>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
        {/* Generate Button */}
        <button
          onClick={generateAvatar}
          disabled={photos.length < 5 || generating}
          className="w-full mt-6 bg-ocean text-white py-3 rounded-ocean disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-ocean-secondary transition"
          data-testid="button-generate-avatar"
        >
          {generating ? 'ğŸŸ¡ Generating...' : 'âœ¨ Generate Avatar'}
        </button>
      </div>
      {/* CENTER PANEL - 3D Preview */}
      <div className="flex-1 bg-ocean-gradient">
        <Canvas camera={{ position: [0, 1.5, 3], fov: 50 }}>
          <ambientLight intensity={0.5} />
          <directionalLight position={[5, 5, 5]} intensity={1} />
          <pointLight position={[-5, 5, -5]} intensity={0.5} />
          
          {generatedAvatarUrl && (
            <PresentationControls
              global
              zoom={0.8}
              rotation={[0, 0, 0]}
              polar={[-Math.PI / 4, Math.PI / 4]}
              azimuth={[-Math.PI / 2, Math.PI / 2]}
            >
              {/* Load generated 3D model */}
              <primitive object={generatedAvatarUrl} />
            </PresentationControls>
          )}
          
          <OrbitControls />
        </Canvas>
      </div>
      {/* RIGHT PANEL - Mr Blue AI Chat */}
      <div className="w-96">
        <MrBlueChat
          context="avatar-designer"
          initialMessage="Hi! I'm here to help you create your perfect 3D avatar. Upload some photos to get started!"
          onClose={() => setMrBlueOpen(false)}
          voiceEnabled={true} // Text AND audio conversations
        />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
async function validatePhotos(photos: File[]) {
  // Agent #76: Quality Validator
  const response = await apiRequest('/api/avatar/validate-photos', {
    method: 'POST',
    body: JSON.stringify({
      photoCount: photos.length,
      // Send metadata for validation
    }),
  });
  
  return await response.json();
}
function fileToBase64(file: File): Promise<string> {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => resolve(reader.result as string);
    reader.onerror = reject;
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  });
}

// FILE: client/src/components/mr-blue/MrBlueChat.tsx
import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Send, Mic, Volume2, VolumeX } from 'lucide-react';
import { MrBlue3DAvatar } from './MrBlue3DAvatar';
import { useWebSpeech } from '@/hooks/use-web-speech';
import { apiRequest } from '@/lib/queryClient';
interface Props {
  context: string;
  initialMessage?: string;
  onClose?: () => void;
  voiceEnabled?: boolean;
}
export function MrBlueChat({ context, initialMessage, onClose, voiceEnabled = true }: Props) {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Array<{ role: 'user' | 'assistant'; content: string }>>([
    { role: 'assistant', content: initialMessage || 'How can I help you today?' },
  ]);
  const [input, setInput] = useState('');
  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);
  const [audioEnabled, setAudioEnabled] = useState(true);
  
  const {
    isListening,
    transcript,
    startListening,
    stopListening,
    speak,
    stopSpeaking,
  } = useWebSpeech();
  // Send message to Mr Blue AI
  const sendMessage = async (text: string) => {
    const userMessage = { role: 'user' as const, content: text };
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, userMessage]);
    setInput('');
    try {
      // Call OpenAI API via backend
      const response = await apiRequest('/api/mr-blue/chat', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: JSON.stringify({
          context,
          messages: [...messages, userMessage],
        }),
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      const assistantMessage = { role: 'assistant' as const, content: data.response };
      
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, assistantMessage]);
      // Text-to-Speech if audio enabled
      if (audioEnabled && voiceEnabled) {
        setIsSpeaking(true);
        await speak(data.response);
        setIsSpeaking(false);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Mr Blue chat error:', error);
    }
  };
  // Voice input
  const handleVoiceInput = () => {
    if (isListening) {
      stopListening();
      if (transcript) {
        sendMessage(transcript);
      }
    } else {
      startListening();
    }
  };
  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-glass-card">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="p-4 border-b border-ocean-divider flex items-center justify-between">
        <h3 className="font-heading-ocean text-ocean">ğŸ¤– Mr Blue</h3>
        {onClose && (
          <button onClick={onClose} className="text-ocean-muted hover:text-ocean">
            âœ•
          </button>
        )}
      </div>
      {/* 3D Avatar */}
      <div className="h-64 bg-ocean-light">
        <MrBlue3DAvatar 
          isAnimating={isSpeaking}
          animation={isSpeaking ? 'talking' : 'idle'}
        />
      </div>
      {/* Chat Messages */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-4">
        {messages.map((msg, index) => (
          <div
            key={index}
            className={`flex ${msg.role === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}
          >
            <div
              className={`max-w-xs px-4 py-2 rounded-lg ${
                msg.role === 'user'
                  ? 'bg-ocean text-white'
                  : 'bg-seafoam text-ocean'
              }`}
              data-testid={`mr-blue-message-${index}`}
            >
              {msg.content}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
      {/* Input Area */}
      <div className="p-4 border-t border-ocean-divider">
        {isListening && (
          <div className="mb-2 p-2 bg-red-50 rounded-lg">
            <p className="text-sm text-red-600">ğŸ”´ Listening...</p>
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{transcript}</p>
          </div>
        )}
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <input
            type="text"
            value={input}
            onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && input && sendMessage(input)}
            placeholder="Type your message..."
            className="flex-1 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg border border-ocean-divider focus:outline-ocean"
            data-testid="input-mr-blue-chat"
          />
          
          {voiceEnabled && (
            <button
              onClick={handleVoiceInput}
              className={`p-2 rounded-lg transition ${
                isListening ? 'bg-red-500 text-white' : 'bg-ocean text-white'
              }`}
              data-testid="button-voice-input"
            >
              <Mic className="w-5 h-5" />
            </button>
          )}
          <button
            onClick={() => sendMessage(input)}
            disabled={!input}
            className="p-2 bg-ocean text-white rounded-lg disabled:opacity-50"
            data-testid="button-send-message"
          >
            <Send className="w-5 h-5" />
          </button>
          {voiceEnabled && (
            <button
              onClick={() => setAudioEnabled(!audioEnabled)}
              className="p-2 bg-glass rounded-lg"
              data-testid="button-toggle-audio"
            >
              {audioEnabled ? <Volume2 className="w-5 h-5" /> : <VolumeX className="w-5 h-5" />}
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

FRIEND REQUEST WORKFLOW IMPLEMENTATION
// FILE: client/src/pages/Friends.tsx
import { useState } from 'react';
import { useQuery, useMutation } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { apiRequest, queryClient } from '@/lib/queryClient';
import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from '@/components/ui/tabs';
import { FriendRequestModal } from '@/components/friends/FriendRequestModal';
import { AcceptRequestModal } from '@/components/friends/AcceptRequestModal';
export default function FriendsPage() {
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('all');
  const [selectedUser, setSelectedUser] = useState<any>(null);
  const [showRequestModal, setShowRequestModal] = useState(false);
  const [showAcceptModal, setShowAcceptModal] = useState(false);
  // Fetch all friends
  const { data: friends, isLoading } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['/api/friends'],
  });
  // Fetch pending requests
  const { data: pendingRequests } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['/api/friends/requests/pending'],
  });
  // Fetch sent requests
  const { data: sentRequests } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['/api/friends/requests/sent'],
  });
  // Send friend request mutation
  const sendRequestMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (data: any) => {
      return apiRequest('/api/friends/request', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: JSON.stringify(data),
      });
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['/api/friends'] });
      setShowRequestModal(false);
    },
  });
  // Accept friend request mutation
  const acceptRequestMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (data: any) => {
      return apiRequest(`/api/friends/request/${data.requestId}/accept`, {
        method: 'POST',
        body: JSON.stringify(data),
      });
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['/api/friends'] });
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['/api/friends/requests/pending'] });
      setShowAcceptModal(false);
    },
  });
  return (
    <div className="container-ocean py-8">
      <h1 className="text-4xl font-heading-ocean mb-6">Friends</h1>
      <Tabs value={activeTab} onValueChange={setActiveTab}>
        <TabsList className="mb-6">
          <TabsTrigger value="all" data-testid="tab-all-friends">
            All Friends ({friends?.length || 0})
          </TabsTrigger>
          <TabsTrigger value="requests" data-testid="tab-requests">
            Requests ({pendingRequests?.length || 0})
          </TabsTrigger>
          <TabsTrigger value="sent" data-testid="tab-sent">
            Sent ({sentRequests?.length || 0})
          </TabsTrigger>
          <TabsTrigger value="find" data-testid="tab-find-friends">
            Find Friends
          </TabsTrigger>
          <TabsTrigger value="suggested" data-testid="tab-suggested">
            Suggested
          </TabsTrigger>
        </TabsList>
        {/* All Friends Tab */}
        <TabsContent value="all">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
            {friends?.map((friend: any) => (
              <FriendCard key={friend.id} friend={friend} />
            ))}
          </div>
        </TabsContent>
        {/* Pending Requests Tab */}
        <TabsContent value="requests">
          <div className="space-y-6">
            {pendingRequests?.map((request: any) => (
              <FriendRequestCard
                key={request.id}
                request={request}
                onAccept={() => {
                  setSelectedUser(request);
                  setShowAcceptModal(true);
                }}
                onDecline={() => {}}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        </TabsContent>
        {/* Other tabs... */}
      </Tabs>
      {/* Modals */}
      {showRequestModal && (
        <FriendRequestModal
          user={selectedUser}
          onSubmit={(data) => sendRequestMutation.mutate(data)}
          onClose={() => setShowRequestModal(false)}
        />
      )}
      {showAcceptModal && (
        <AcceptRequestModal
          request={selectedUser}
          onAccept={(data) => acceptRequestMutation.mutate(data)}
          onClose={() => setShowAcceptModal(false)}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

IMPLEMENTATION CODE
// FILE: client/src/pages/admin/VisualEditor.tsx
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Monaco } from '@monaco-editor/react';
import { useQuery, useMutation } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { apiRequest, queryClient } from '@/lib/queryClient';
import { AdaptiveButton } from '@/components/adaptive/AdaptiveButton';
import { AdaptiveCard } from '@/components/adaptive/AdaptiveCard';
import { useToast } from '@/hooks/use-toast';
export default function VisualEditor() {
  const [pageName, setPageName] = useState('');
  const [routePath, setRoutePath] = useState('');
  const [description, setDescription] = useState('');
  const [permissions, setPermissions] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [reviewComplete, setReviewComplete] = useState(false);
  const [code, setCode] = useState('');
  const [previewMode, setPreviewMode] = useState<'desktop' | 'mobile' | 'tablet'>('desktop');
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState<'light' | 'dark'>('light');
  const [aiPrompt, setAiPrompt] = useState('');
  const { toast } = useToast();
  // AI Code Generation
  const generateCodeMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (prompt: string) => {
      return apiRequest('/api/ai/generate-code', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: JSON.stringify({
          prompt,
          context: 'visual-editor',
          model: 'gpt-4o',
        }),
      });
    },
    onSuccess: (data) => {
      setCode(data.code);
      toast({
        title: "Code Generated!",
        description: `Cost: $${data.cost.toFixed(3)} â€¢ Time: ${data.time}s`,
      });
    },
  });
  // Save page mutation
  const savePageMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (data: any) => {
      return apiRequest('/api/admin/pages', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: JSON.stringify(data),
      });
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      toast({
        title: "Page Saved",
        description: reviewComplete ? "Marked as Review Complete" : "Saved as draft",
      });
      
      if (reviewComplete) {
        // Update "The Plan" document
        updateThePlan();
      }
    },
  });
  // AI pre-fill suggestions based on route
  useEffect(() => {
    if (routePath.startsWith('/admin')) {
      setPermissions(['Admin', 'Super Admin', 'God Mode']);
    } else if (routePath.startsWith('/events')) {
      setPermissions(['Registered Users']);
    } else {
      setPermissions(['Public']);
    }
  }, [routePath]);
  return (
    <div className="h-screen flex flex-col">
      {/* Top Bar */}
      <div className="h-16 bg-ocean text-white flex items-center justify-between px-6">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold">Visual Editor (Agent #78)</h1>
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <AdaptiveButton variant="secondary" onClick={() => savePageMutation.mutate({ ...pageData, draft: true })}>
            Save Draft
          </AdaptiveButton>
          <AdaptiveButton onClick={() => savePageMutation.mutate({ ...pageData, publish: true })}>
            Publish to Production
          </AdaptiveButton>
        </div>
      </div>
      {/* 4-Panel Layout */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex overflow-hidden">
        {/* LEFT PANEL */}
        <div className="w-1/4 bg-glass-card overflow-y-auto border-r border-ocean-divider">
          <div className="p-4">
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-4">Page Settings</h2>
            
            {/* Page Name */}
            <label className="block mb-2">
              <span className="text-sm font-medium">Page Name</span>
              <input
                type="text"
                value={pageName}
                onChange={(e) => setPageName(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full mt-1 px-3 py-2 border rounded-ocean"
                placeholder="e.g., Event Detail Page"
              />
            </label>
            {/* Route Path */}
            <label className="block mb-2">
              <span className="text-sm font-medium">Route Path</span>
              <input
                type="text"
                value={routePath}
                onChange={(e) => setRoutePath(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full mt-1 px-3 py-2 border rounded-ocean"
                placeholder="/events/:id"
              />
            </label>
            {/* User Permissions - MULTI-SELECT */}
            <div className="mb-4">
              <span className="text-sm font-medium">User Type Permissions</span>
              <div className="mt-2 space-y-2">
                {['Public', 'Registered Users', 'Paid Users', 'PRO Users', 'Admin', 'Super Admin', 'God Mode'].map((type) => (
                  <label key={type} className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <input
                      type="checkbox"
                      checked={permissions.includes(type)}
                      onChange={(e) => {
                        if (e.target.checked) {
                          setPermissions([...permissions, type]);
                        } else {
                          setPermissions(permissions.filter(p => p !== type));
                        }
                      }}
                    />
                    <span className="text-sm">{type}</span>
                  </label>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
            {/* Review Complete Checkbox */}
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 p-3 bg-seafoam-light rounded-ocean">
              <input
                type="checkbox"
                checked={reviewComplete}
                onChange={(e) => setReviewComplete(e.target.checked)}
                data-testid="checkbox-review-complete"
              />
              <span className="text-sm font-semibold">â­ Review Complete</span>
            </label>
            
            {reviewComplete && (
              <div className="mt-2 p-2 bg-green-50 rounded-ocean text-sm text-green-700">
                âœ… Will update "The Plan" & enable production publish
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
        {/* CENTER PANEL - Monaco Editor */}
        <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col">
          <Monaco
            height="100%"
            language="typescript"
            theme={theme === 'dark' ? 'vs-dark' : 'light'}
            value={code}
            onChange={(value) => setCode(value || '')}
            options={{
              minimap: { enabled: false },
              fontSize: 14,
              wordWrap: 'on',
            }}
          />
        </div>
        {/* RIGHT PANEL - Preview */}
        <div className="w-1/4 bg-gray-50 flex flex-col">
          <div className="p-2 border-b flex gap-2">
            <button onClick={() => setPreviewMode('desktop')}>ğŸ’» Desktop</button>
            <button onClick={() => setPreviewMode('mobile')}>ğŸ“± Mobile</button>
            <button onClick={() => setTheme(theme === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light')}>
              {theme === 'light' ? 'ğŸŒ™' : 'â˜€ï¸'}
            </button>
          </div>
          
          <iframe
            srcDoc={`<html><body>${code}</body></html>`}
            className="flex-1 border-0"
            style={{
              width: previewMode === 'mobile' ? '375px' : '100%',
              margin: previewMode === 'mobile' ? '0 auto' : '0',
            }}
          />
        </div>
      </div>
      {/* BOTTOM PANEL - AI Chat */}
      <div className="h-1/6 bg-glass border-t border-ocean-divider p-4">
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <input
            type="text"
            value={aiPrompt}
            onChange={(e) => setAiPrompt(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Ask AI to generate code..."
            className="flex-1 px-3 py-2 border rounded-ocean"
            onKeyDown={(e) => {
              if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                generateCodeMutation.mutate(aiPrompt);
              }
            }}
          />
          <AdaptiveButton
            onClick={() => generateCodeMutation.mutate(aiPrompt)}
            disabled={generateCodeMutation.isPending}
          >
            {generateCodeMutation.isPending ? 'Generating...' : 'Generate'}
          </AdaptiveButton>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
